From the outstanding service to the Hurst burger that ordered another one on a side order, to the NY-style cheesecake that I had to fight over with my friend, this restaurant is very understated. Sweet potato fries were great, chicken fingers were 7 large pieces.

So glad I stopped in here! Nice, although a bit distant, ocean views were a bonus. Worth the stop.</text>

<Rating>4<//Rating><text>The Cavalier Restaurant, part of the Cavalier Oceanfront Resort, is located on the north end of the property, where the views of the Pacific are not to be believed. Breakfast through dinner service is available.

The eatery offers a good selection of popular American restaurant foods: pastas, meats, chickens, fish, potatoes, and salads. Several vegan items are available. The chef will attempt to modify recipes to meet your dietary requirements. Many beers and local wines are served. Non alcoholic beer available.

Service is friendly and knowledgeable at this large, busy restaurant. The decor is comfortable.  Warm rolls, delivered to the table, are served with butter. I asked for and received balsamic vinegar and olive oil. Servings are resort large and mildly spiced.

This eatery is a favorite of locals. Several locals in Cambria mention the restaurant.  At dinner time, the restaurant can be quite busy. It's best to make a reservation.

Parking is free and easy. Everything is wheelchair accessible. Morning newspapers, from up and down the coast, are available just outside the restaurant. Since the papers are delivered by truck, sometimes, due to fog or whatever, they're a bit late.< /text>< pics>

<Pics>None< /Pics>< review>
Summary: Nice and friendly service, good take out container, good location, and bland and tasteless food.

Got a burger with coleslaw. It was just so disappointing bland and without any flavour. Save yourself the disappointment and try to see if something is open down the road in Cambria. I wish I had. I was desperate for a warm meal of any kind after eight hours of travel and I had adequate expectations for the food I could expect in a very small highway stop.

Unfortunately the reality felt way short of that. The burger was cooked well enough but there was just so little flavour to anything, even with added cheese and grilled mushrooms...extra price I paid to ensure some sort of deliciousness. Nope. The coleslaw was quite poor as well. No seasoning. No mayo or vinaigrette to add some taste. Just shredded cabbage.

The positive was that the price was decently reasonable at $14 plus a couple bucks for premium toppings given this was a captive audience in the middle of a couple hotels. However the meal was so poor I felt like I just paid to fill myself instead of getting any enjoyment. At least a fast food burger should give you a few minutes of pleasure for the few bucks.

Also positive was the gentleman helping me place my order. Very nice guy and professional. Service was quick as well and the take out packaging was great.< /review>

To be honest at first I thought this was going to be one of those thing that'll be good only for a few day and then I would end up paying for something else just to keep it clean, but I was wrong. I am super glad I went with the DFI treatment cause it really makes a huge difference. After the install and using the shower for 3 weeks I started noticing the glass was starting to haze because of the water droplets and soap residue. So I read what DFI recommended which was really simple, just use a soft cloth and go over the surface in circular motion and then rinse (no cleaner just water). I really couldn't believe it, I really thought this was BS but to my surprise it really worked shower glass looks like new again. The haze, droplets and soap residue all gone. < text>
Home Brewer? Beer snob? Industry personnel with a beer emergency? Scott at Windsor has got you covered.

Whether you're just getting started or a serious home Brewer, Windsor carries all the homebrew supplies you could possibly want. Looking for so thing specific? Talk to Scott. He's quite often happy to oblige.

Beer snob looking to learn more about where your beer comes from? Be sure to check out Windsor's events- you'll find many of southern California's top craft brewers stopping by to chat about their industry.

Or, if you're like me and finding your beer on the go setup kind of lacking (jockey box missing some attachments), or your CO2 tank needs to be filled, let Windsor help you out.

Call ahead if you're on the hunt for something special, you'll know before you go!< /text>

<Date>1582852442036</Date><rating>5< /rating><review>Simple is more.
This is my new favorite chicken wing joint at the moment!

Dispite only having 3 flavors, each flavor is equally delicious. Soy Garlic and Sweet Spicy is tied for my favorite. The breading of the chicken wings are also delicious. The flavors enhance the breading. The wings are also meaty! Each wing is consistent with flavoring, breading, and meatiness.

The fries are the perfect compliment to the wings. They remind me of McDonalds fries. For me, I love the fries. Theh compliment the flavors just as well as the wings do.

Staff has always been pleasant, and happy. I've made several complicated orders for coworkers, and the staff is always helpful.

Haven't tried all food menu items, however this place easily earned my 5 stars!</review>< pics>
